e
 june-july

 The India Today anti-fake News War Room (AFWA) found that the post being viral has nothing to do with any school in India
 ye aadesh pakistan ke sindh hoicourt ne jari kiya tha
 The archived version of the post can be seen here
 fasebuk pej 'sat samachar jind' ne ek patr kii tasviir post kii he

 "by the time the news was written, this post had been shared more than 73000 times

 viral ho rahaa ye order 'krime intelligence detective' ke letrehad par chapa hua dikhataa he
 AFWA found out that 'crime Intelligence Detective' is an NGO working against corruption
 letterhed par enjio kaa pataa or helpline number dekha ja saktaa he
 Below this letter is written 'director General, Crime Intelligence Detective (india)', but no name has been written on it

 Eight senior leaders were inducted into the United Progressive Alliance (UPA) government headed by Prime Minister Manmohan Singh on Monday in view of the assembly elections to be held in five states at the end of the year
 is badlaav ko haalanki khaas prabhavi nahin mana ja rahaa he, kyonki nae chehron main yuva nahin, balki varishthatam ko mantrimandal main laayaa gaya he
 Even in the general election, there is less than a year, which is why Manmohan Singh has clearly adopted a safe path and brought only those who have a better record within the party
 somvaar ko kendriya mantrimandal main shaamil kiye aath mantriyon main sabase yuva mantri kii umr 59 varsh he, jabaki rajasthan ke varisht netaa 86 varshiya sheesh ram ola sabase bujurg netaa hai
 There was speculation that the Congress would give young faces a berth in the cabinet but all speculation was dismissed
 samprag-2 ke kaarykaal main yah chauthaa bada pherbadal he
 All the ministers inducted in the cabinet are believed to be confidant of Sonia Gandhi, while it was expected that some of Rahul Gandhi's core team may be included
 cabinet mantri ke rup main shaamil kiye jane waalon main shishram ola (shram mantri), auskar fernadis (sadak yatayaat evam rajmarg mantri), girija vyas (awaas evam garibi unmoolan mantri) evam kees raav (kapadaa mantri) hai
 Apart from this, Manik Rao Gavit (social Justice and Empowerment), Santosh Chaudhary (health), EMS Nachiappan (commerce and Industry) and JD Salem (finance) have been included as Ministers of State
 seepi joshi party sanghathan se judane ke liye mantri pad chhod chuke hai, isliye varishthatam congressi mallikarjun khadge ko shram mantri pad se hataakar rail mantri banaaya gaya he
 Ola and Vyas are the leaders of Rajasthan in the cabinet
 dhyaan rahe ki rajasthan main varsh ke aakhir main vidhansabha chunaav hone hai
 After the swearing-in ceremony at Rashtrapati Bhavan on Monday, the Prime Minister hoped that the UPA would be able to return to power for the third time
 manmohan singh ne kaha, "meraa hameshaa se maananaa rahaa he ki samprag teesri baar bhi satta main aegi or janata ham par dobaaraa apana vishwaas jataayegi
 " manmohan singh ne is baat ko bhi doharaaya ki vah rahul gandhi ko apane pad par dekhakar bahut khush honge
 This reshuffle in the UPA cabinet comes just a day after the organizational renewal in the Congress and the age of the ministers involved becomes important because the newly appointed General Secretary of the Congress, Ajay Maken, said that there is a young India at the center of the Congress, which has 60 per cent The population is over 30 years old
 kendriya mantrimandal main pherbadal ke fouran baad pramukh vipakshi dal bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ne chutki lete hue kaha ki yah ek maranasann pherbadal he
 BJP spokesperson Nirmala Sitharaman said, "this is a dead shuffle
 congress iske jariye apane varisht netaaon ko izzat pradaan karnaa chaahati he
 "comments bhartiya communist party (bhakpa) ke netaa di
 Raja said that since many constituents had left the Congress, this reshuffle was necessary
 pichley varsh november main mantrimandal main hue pherbadal ko haalanki manmohan singh ne aam chunaav se pehle sambhavat: aakhri pherbadal kaha tha, lekin uske baad dravid munetra kadgam (diemke) tathaa trinmul congress ke samprag se alag ho jane ke kaaran tathaa vivaad ke kaaran purv rail mantri pawan kumaar bansal tathaa purv kanoon mantri ashvini kumaar ko apane-apane padon se istipha dene ke kaaran somvaar ko kiya gaya pherbadal jaruri ho gaya tha

 The youngest minister is 59 years old among the eight ministers inducted into the Union Cabinet on Monday, while the senior leader of Rajasthan, 86-year-old Sheesh Ram Ola, is the eldest
 atakalein lagaai ja rahi thim ki congress yuva chehron ko mantrimandal main jagah degi lekin sabhi atakalein khaarij ho gayi
 This is the fourth major reshuffle during upa-ii's tenure
 mantrimandal main shaamil kiye gaye sabhi mantriyon ko sonia gandhi kaa vishwaasapaatr mana ja rahaa he, jabaki ummid thi ki rahul gandhi kii kor team main se kuch logon ko shaamil kiya ja saktaa he
 Among those who have been inducted as Cabinet Ministers are Sesharam Ola (labor Minister), Oscar Fernandes (minister of Road Transport and Highways), Girija Vyas (minister for Housing and Poverty Alleviation) and KS Rao (textile Minister)
 iske alaava rajya mantri ke rup main maanik raav gavit (samaajik nyaay evam adhikarita), santosh choudhary (swasthya), iemes nachiappan (vaanijya evam udyog) or jedy selem (vitt) ko shaamil kiya gaya he
 CP Joshi has left the ministerial post to join the party organization, so the senior-most Congress Mallikarjun Kharge has been removed from the post of Labor Minister and made the Railway Minister
 mantrimandal main shaamil hone waalon main ola or vyas rajasthan ke dhakad netaa hai
 Keep in mind that Rajasthan elections are to be held at the end of the year
 raashtrapati bhawan main somvaar ko shapath grahan samaaroh ke baad pradhanmantri ne aashaa vyakt kii ki samprag teesri baar bhi satta main vaapasi karne main safal rahegi
 Manmohan Singh said, "I have always believed that the UPA will come to power for the third time and the people will repose their faith in us again
 " Manmohan Singh also reiterated that he would be very happy to see Rahul Gandhi in his post

 Political Background: The politics of Marwar in Rajasthan has been dominated by the Mirdha family since independence
 sabase baldevaraam mirdha ne kisaanon ke hiton kii raksha ke liye marwar kisaan sabha sthapana kii
 But the country's first Prime Minister Pt
 jawaharlal nehru se madhyastata ke baad kisaan sabha kaa congress main vilay ho gaya
 After this, Ramdevas Mirdha, son of Baldev Ram Mirdha and Nathuram Mirdha of his own family, dominated the politics here for almost six decades
 lekin dhire-dhire mirdha parivaar kaa asar kam hone laga
 So now the new generation is seen struggling to save this political legacy
 pichley kuch samay se do pramukh dal congress or bijepi ke bich ek nae khilaadi ke taur par hanuman beniwal ubhare hai jo jat yuvaaon ko saath lekar is donon dalon se alag lakeer khichna chaahate hai
 After independence, Congress won the maximum number of 16 general elections and 2 by-elections in Nagaur Lok Sabha seat from 1952 to 2014, 11 times
 1952 main nirdaleey ummidavaar jidi somani jite
 Mathura Das of Congress in 1957, NK Somani of Congress in 1960 by-election and Surendra Kumar Dey of Congress in 1962 were elected from here
 lekin 1967 main congress ke enke somani swatantri party ke tikat par chunaav jeet
 After this, the Mirdha family continued to hold this seat from 1971 to 1997
 1971 main nathuram mirdha yahaan ke saansad chune gaye
 So at the Janata wave of 1977, Nathuram Mirdha managed to save this seat
 1980 main nathuram mirdha congress (you) ke tikat par yahaan ke saansad bane
 An interesting contest was witnessed in this seat in 1984 when Ramdivas Mirdha and Nathuram Mirdha, two strong leaders of the Mirdha family, pitted against each other
 is chunaav main congress ke tikat par ramanivas mirdha ne bhartiya lokdal se ummidavaar nathuram mirdha ko shikast di
 But in the 1989 election, Nathuram Mirdha defeated Ram Niwas Mirdha while contesting from the Janata Dal
 iske 1991 or 1996 ke loksabhaa chunaav main kagress ke tikat par nathuram mirdha kaa is seat par kabja rahaa
 But after the death of Nathuram Mirdha, his son Bhanuprakash Mirdha won the seat on the BJP ticket in 1997 bypoll defeating Ram Niwas Mirdha of Congress
 yah pehla mauka tha jab bijepi ne is seat par jeet kaa swaad chakhaa, lekin party ko sahaara mirdha parivaar kaa hi lenaa padaa
 So far, Ram Raghunath Chaudhary entered Nagaur politics revolving around the Mirdha family
 mana jaataa he ki mirdha parivaar kii aapasi foot kii vajah se ramaraghunatha choudhary yahaan kii siyasat main apni jagah banane main kaamyaab rahen
 In 1998 and 1999, Ram Raghunath Chaudhary was elected MP for two consecutive terms on Congress ticket
 lekin choudhary saal 2004 main bijepi ke bhavar singh dangavas se chunaav haar gaye

 lekin 2014 kii modi lahar main jyoti mirdha yah seat bachaane main naakaamayaab raheen or bijepi ke siaar choudhary nagaur ke saansad chune gaye
 The Social tana-bananagaur Lok Sabha constituency consists of 8 out of 10 assembly seats in the district, while two of the Legislative Assembly Merta and Degana are included in Rajsamand Lok Sabha
 bhugolic drushtikon se nagaur jila bikaner or jodhpur ke madhya main sthit rajasthan kaa paanchavaa sabase bada jila he

 vahiin anusuchit jati kii aabaadi bhi apana mahatv rakhti he

 64 pratishat hissaa shahari or 20
 36 percent is rural
 vahiin kul aabaadi kaa 20
 91 percent are Scheduled Castes
 2014 loksabhaa chunaav ke aankadon ke mutabik nagaur sansadeey seat matadaataaon kii kul sankhya 16,78,662 he, jisamen se 8,86,731 purush or 7,91,931 mahila matadaata hai

 jabaki congress ne 6 seat par jeet kaa paracham laharaaya

 Report card of MP 70 year old Nagaur MP CR Chaudhary was born on 1 March 1948 in Nagaur
 unhone apni snatakottar kii degree rajasthan uniwarsity se hasil karne ke baad england kii birmingham uniwarsity se gramin vikaas ke kshetra main training lee
 CR Chaudhary served as a college lecturer from 1971 to 1977 in Dausa, Sirohi and Ajmer
 lekin 1978 main unka chayan rajasthan prashasnic seva main hua
 He was promoted to the Indian Administrative Service in the years 2001–2002
 apane kaarykaal ke dauraan choudhary ne vibhinn prashasnic padon par seva di

 isse pehle vijay bahuguna ne kaha tha ki main hi uttarakhand kaa mukhyamantri banuunga
 Bahuguna said that today only he will take oath of office while his cabinet will take oath later
 isse pehle yah khabaren aa rahi thi ki harish ravat ke virodh ke baad shapathgrahan ko ek din ke liye taala ja saktaa he
 The comments harish ravat mukhyamantri na banaaye jane se bahut khafa hai
 Anger of resentment is that he has sent his resignation to Congress leader Sonia Gandhi
 vahiin, vijay bahuguna ko mukhyamantri banaae jane ko lekar ab congress do bhaagon main banty nazar aa rahi he
 Annoyed at not being made the Chief Minister, Harak Singh Rawat of Uttarakhand Congress has also come along with Harish Rawat
 unhone saaf kaha he ki bahuguna ko siem banane kaa faisalaa galat he or yah sarkaar zyada din nahin chalegi
 At the same time, BJP is trying to take advantage of the growing schism in the Congress
 yah khabaren bhi aa rahi hai ki harish ravat bijepi ke netaaon se sampark banaae hue hai
 At the same time, the party high command has called Nishank to Delhi so that a consensus can be reached

 At the same time, the party high command has called Nishank to Delhi so that a consensus can be reached
 vahiin congress main badhati foot kaa phayda uthaane kii koshish bijepi kar rahi he
 There are also reports that Harish Rawat is in touch with BJP leaders
 vahiin party alaakaman ne nishank ko dilli bulaayaa he taaki kisi aam sahmati tak pahunchaa ja sake
 India on Sunday test-fired the nuclear-powered Agni-2 strategic ballistic missile from a military base in Odisha
 bharat kar rahaa he agni-6 missile kaa vikassutron ne bataaya ki pareekshan bhubaneshwar se kareeb 200 kilometre dur bhadrak jile me whealer dweep se kiya gaya
 The military personnel tested it as a training exercise
 tasveeron main jaaniye bharat kii missile shaktisatah se sataha par maar karne vaali madhyam duuri kii is missile ko pehle hi sena main shaamil kiya ja chukaa he
 Its firepower is more than 2,000 km
 yah parmaanu hamale ko rokane se sambandhit ranneetik sainya shastraagaar kaa hissaa he
 Veteran England cricket team player Ben Stokes said in his defense during the hearing of the disputed case in Bristol court that he did whatever he could to protect himself and those around him
 bibisi kii report ke anusaar, bristol vivaad main shaamil stokes lords main jari duusare test match ke liye england team main shaamil nahin hai
 It is noteworthy that Stokes has a case of assault with people outside a nightclub in Bristol
 is maamle par bristol kii ek adaalat main sunwaayee jari he
 During the hearing, Stokes was asked about his first reaction to the violence, saying that Ryan Ali was trying to attack him with a bottle in his hand
 indvseng: barish ke khalal tak bharat kaa score 11 / 2, kohli or pujaara krij parstokes ne kaha, 'main apana or apane aasapaas shaamil logon kaa bachaav kar rahaa tha
 Because of this he joined this fight
 maine jo bhi kiya uskaa faisla behad jaldi liya
 i understood that these two people (ali and Ryan Hale) could also threaten the rest of the people
 'england ke khilaadi ne kaha, 'maine jo kuch bhi kiya apane bachaav main kiya
 i was feeling threatened by both these people
 main nashe main nahin tha
 ' dilli main mukhyamantri-uparajyapal ke bich badhate takaraav ko 'ahm' kaa maamla bataate hue aap ke nishkasit netaa yogendra yadav ne shanivaar ko mukhyamantri arvind kejariwal par vaastavik muddon se behad aparipakv tareeke se nipatane ke liye nishaanaa saadhaa
 Yadav, who started a political campaign 'swaraj Abhiyan' after being ousted from the AAP due to differences with the top leadership, also said that now he has decided not to form a political party
 unhone kaha ki vah aap par focus nahin kar rahe hai jo mahaj ek kshetreey party he, balki unka manch desh main vaikalpik raajnneeti ko majboot karne kii koshish kar rahaa he or yah bihar or kuch anya chunavi rajyon main kuch ummidavaaron kaa samarthan kar saktaa he
 His organization is uniting people feeling 'cheated' by the developments in AAP
 unhone kaha ki dilli sarkaar kii shaktiyon ke mudde par kejariwal ne jo niti apanaai he vah pratikul prabhaav daalane vaali he
 Without naming Kejriwal, Yadav said, 'I think the very real issue is being raised in a very immature way
 ' unhone kaha, 'dilli ko purna rajya hona chahie
 An elected government of Delhi should have the right to appoint and transfer officers like any other elected government
 durbhaagya he ki hamaara samvidhan or kanoon abhi isaki ijaajat nahin detaa
 ' yadav ne kaha, 'jahaan ham the or jahaan hamen hona chahie usamen badlaav bahut dhairya, baatcheet or vinamrata se honi chahie
 ' yadav ne kaha, 'durbhaagya se ham jo dekh rahe hai vah takaraav he, ahm kaa takaraav, asthirataa he
 i am afraid that dealing with real issues in this way will prove to be adversely affected
 ' puche jane par ki khud ko party se baahar kiye jane par kya unhen koi afsos he, unhone kaha, 'yah kahana morrkhtaa hoga ki mujhe koi pachhtaawaa nahin he, yah kahana bevakoofi hogi ki mujhe is tarah dhakke khaanaa pasand he or yah nasamajhi hogi ki is tarah se pachhtaawaa karte hue jindagi guzari jaae
 ' unhone kaha ki raajnneeti main pehali baar pravesh karne vaale lakhon log thaga hua mahasoos kar rahe hai or swaraj andolan ke jariye unhen saath laayaa ja rahaa he or desh main vaikalpik raajnneeti ke prati ek baar unamem phir ummiden jaagi hai
 Referring to the platform role initiated by him and another expelled leader of AAP, Prashant Bhushan, Yadav said, 'swaraj Abhiyan is an attempt to strengthen alternative politics in the country, but politics is not our aim to contest elections and This is not how to form a government
 ' He said, 'as of now we are not a political party, so there is no question of contesting elections in Bihar as a Swaraj campaign
 ' But because we are a political movement, we are committed to interfere in the democratic process
 tippaniyan He said, 'and we can do this by giving an alternative agenda, spreading public awareness and opposing tainted candidates and exposing irregularities in elections
 unhone kaha, 'kuch chuninda maamalon main ham praayogic taur par un kuch ummidavaaron kaa samarthan kar sakate hai jo kisi raajnneetik dal se jude hue nahin hai
 ' sheersh netritv ke saath matbhed saream hone par aap se baahar kiye jane ke baad raajnneetik muhim 'swaraj abhiyaan' chalaane vaale yadav ne yah bhi kaha ki ab unhone raajnneetik dal nahin banane kaa faisla kiya he
 He said that he is not focusing on AAP which is just a regional party, but his platform is trying to strengthen alternative politics in the country and it can support some candidates in Bihar and some other electoral states
 aap main ghatnakramon se 'thaga hua' mahasoos kar rahe logon ko unka sanghathan ekajute kar rahaa he
 He said that the policy adopted by Kejriwal on the issue of Delhi Government's powers is going to adversely affect it
 kejariwal kaa naam liye bina yadav ne kaha, 'mujhe lagata he ki bahut vaastavik mudde ko bahut hi aparipakv tareeke se uthaaya ja rahaa he
 'he said,' Delhi should be a full state
 dilli kii ek nirvaachit sarkaar ke paas kisi bhi anya nirvaachit sarkaar kii tarah adhikariyon kii niyukti or sthanantaran kaa adhikaar hona chahie
 Unfortunately, our constitution and law do not allow this
 ' Yadav said, 'the change in where we were and where we should be should be done with great patience, conversation and humility
 ' Yadav said, 'unfortunately what we are seeing is a confrontation, an important confrontation, instability
 mujhe dar he ki vaastavik muddon se is tarah se nipatna pratikul prabhaav daalane vaala sabit hoga
 Asked if he regretted being thrown out of the party, he said, "it would be foolish to say that i have no regrets, it would be stupid to say that i like to eat like this and it would be stupid
" That life should be lived by regretting it in this way
 ' He said that lakhs of people entering politics for the first time are feeling cheated and they are being brought together through the Swaraj movement and once again they have raised hopes for alternative politics in the country
 unke or aap ke ek or nishkasit netaa prashanth bhushan dwaara shuru kiye gaye manch kii bhoomika kaa ullekh karte hue yadav ne kaha, 'swaraj abhiyaan desh main vaikalpik raajnneeti ko majboot karne kii koshish he, lekin hamaare liye raajnneeti chunaav ladane kaa lakshya nahin he or yah nahin ki kaise sarkaar banaai jaae
 ' unhone kaha, 'abhi ke hisaab se ham koi raajnneetik dal nahin hai isliye bihar main swaraj abhiyaan ke taur par chunaav ladane kaa koi sawaal hi nahin he
 ' lekin kyonki ham ek raajnneetik andolan hai isliye ham loktantric prakriya main hastkshep karne ke liye patibaddh hai
 The comments unhone kaha, 'or yah kaam ham ek vaikalpik agenda dekar, jan jaagrukta failaakar or daagi ummidavaaron kaa virodh karke tathaa chunaav main aniyamitataayen ujagar karke kar sakate hai
 He said, 'in select cases, we can experimentally support some candidates who are not associated with any political party
 ' He said that he is not focusing on AAP which is just a regional party, but his platform is trying to strengthen alternative politics in the country and it can support some candidates in Bihar and some other electoral states
